  --- Recto English -----------------------------------------------------
  
  make art
  
  a week dedicated to the world of Free Software and digital art
  
  Poitiers, France
  
  From the 8th to the 13th of December 2009
  
  Exhibition | Concerts | Presentations | Workshop
  
  Aharon Amir (GB), Wayne Clements (GB), FooCorp (GB), Gijs Gieskes (NL),
  Gullibloon (AT/DE), Adnan Hadzi (CH), Lisa Haskel (GB), Reni Hofmüller (AT),
  Olivier Laruelle (FR), LAFKON (DE), Anne Laforêt (FR), Mattin (ES),
  Antoine Moreau (FR), Nathalie Magnan (FR), No Copy Paste (HU), Noyade (Fr),
  Jean Sépulchre (FR), Wesley Smith (US), Koray Tahiroğlu (TR/FI),
  The Guardians of the Tradition (US), Taku Unami (JP), Milovann Yanatchkov (FR),
  Simon Yuill (GB), Jérémie Zimmermann (FR), IOhannes M. Zmölnig (AT), ...
  
  
  --- Verso English -----------------------------------------------------
  
  
  make art is an international festival focussed on Free/Libre/Open Source
  Software (FLOSS) and open content in digital arts. make art offers performances,
  presentations, workshops and an exhibition, focused on the blurred line between
  art and software programming. 



  == What The Fork?! ==
  =====================  

  This year make art focusses on distributed
  and open practices in FLOSS art.
  'What the fork?!' is about decentralization.
  Forking is the new black.
  Work from one source, copy, patch, improve,
  experiment, change direction, inspire!
  Forking is not about quick hacks,
  but about creating room to experiment,
  letting go of the one working copy
  and creating a multiplicity of ideas.

  --- Recto French ------------------------------------------------------
   
  make art
  
  une semaine dédiée aux mondes du Logiciel Libre et des arts numériques
  
  Poitiers, France
  
  Du 8 au 13 décembre 2009
  
  Exposition | Concerts | Présentations | Atelier
  
  Aharon Amir (GB), Wayne Clements (GB), FooCorp (GB), Gijs Gieskes (NL),
  Gullibloon (AT/DE), Adnan Hadzi (CH), Lisa Haskel (GB), Reni Hofmüller (AT),
  Olivier Laruelle (FR), LAFKON (DE), Anne Laforêt (FR), Mattin (ES),
  Antoine Moreau (FR), Nathalie Magnan (FR), No Copy Paste (HU), Noyade (Fr),
  Jean Sépulchre (FR), Wesley Smith (US), Koray Tahiroğlu (TR/FI),
  The Guardians of the Tradition (US), Taku Unami (JP), Milovann Yanatchkov (FR),
  Simon Yuill (GB), Jérémie Zimmermann (FR), IOhannes M. Zmölnig (AT), ... 
  
  
  --- Verso French ------------------------------------------------------
  
  
  make art est un festival international dédié au Logiciel Libre et Open Source (FLOSS*)
  et aux pratiques ouvertes dans les arts numériques. make art propose des performances,
  des présentations, des ateliers et un exposition, situés au croisement de l'art et de
  la programmation de logiciel.
  
  
  
  == What The Fork?! ==
  =====================
    
  Cette année make art est centré sur
  les pratiques distribuées et ouvertes en art FLOSS.
  'What the fork?!' c'est la décentralisation.
  Le fork c'est la nouvelle tendance.
  Travailler à partir d'une source, copier, patcher, améliorer,
  expérimenter, changer de direction, inspirer !
  Le fork, ce n'est pas de simples hacks,
  mais plutôt la création d'un espace d'expérimentation,
  qui laisse de côté la copie unique de travail
  et qui démultiplie les idées.

% ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- %

  #!/bin/bash
  cat <<":*" |
  								_
     _        _     ____     _       _   _______|_|         
    | |_    _| |  _|____|_  | |    _|_| |  _____|           
    |  _|__|_  | | |____| | | |___|_|   | |_____            
    | | |__| | | |  ____  | |  ___|_    |  _____|           
    | |      | | | |_   | | | |   |_|_  | |_______          
    |_|_     |_| |___|  |_| |_|     |_| |_________|         
      |_|_          ____     _______     _________          
        |_|       _|____|_  |  _____|_  |___   ___|_    _   
                 | |____| | | |_____|_|     | |   |_|  |_|  
    08-13 DEC    |  __    | |  _   _|       | |             
    2009         | |  |_  | | | |_|___     _|_|             
    POITIERS     |_|    |_| |_|   |___|   |_|               
   
  
  make art is an international festival dedicated to the integration 
  of Free/Libre/Open Source Software (FLOSS) in digital art.
  
  The fourth edition of make art - What The Fork?! distributed and 
  open practices in FLOSS art - will take place in Poitiers (FR),
  from the 7th to the 13th of December 2009.
  With Aharon Amir (GB), Wayne Clements (GB), FooCorp (GB), Gijs Gieskes (NL),
  Gullibloon (AT), Adnan Hadzi (CH), Reni Hofmüller (AT), Olivier Laruelle (FR),
  LAFKON (DE), Anne Laforêt (FR), Mattin (ES), Milovann Yanatchkov (FR),
  Antoine Moreau (FR), Nathalie Magnan (FR), No Copy Paste (HU), Jean Sépulchre (FR),
  Wesley Smith (US), Koray Tahiroğlu (TR/FI), The Guardians of the Tradition (US),
  Simon Yuill (GB), Jérémie Zimmermann (FR), IOhannes M. Zmölnig (AT)
   
  http://makeart.goto10.org
  
  :*
  
  (
  ( echo '[-]>[-]---------->[-],[----------[>[-]++++++++++,----------]'
    echo '<[++++++++++.<]>++++++++++.-------------------->[-],]' ) | (
  echo '#include <stdio.h>'
  echo '#include <stdlib.h>'
  echo 'int main(int c, char **a){'
  echo 'char *makeart = calloc(2009,1);'
  sed -e 's/+/++*makeart;\n/g' \
      -e 's/-/--*makeart;\n/g' \
      -e 's/>/++makeart;\n/g' \
      -e 's/</--makeart;\n/g' \
      -e 's/\./putchar\(*makeart\);\n/g' \
      -e 's/,/{int i = getchar\(\);if\(i!=EOF\)*makeart=i;}\n/g' \
      -e 's/\[/while\(*makeart\){\n/g' \
      -e 's/\]/}\n/g' \
      -e 't' \
      -e 's/.//g'
  echo 'return 0;}'
  ) | gcc -O2 -Wall -std=c99 -pedantic -o makeart -xc - &&
  ./makeart | ./makeart
  )

  hi thomas & marloes,

  > hopefully you two (who is the second designer?) can find time

  we hope so too ;), we already started with some drafts.
  the other designer is benjamin stephan, one half of lafkon office space.

  some more questions from our side:

  - how do you plan to print the posters? we have been working on a
  generative approach comparable to lac08
  (http://vektordb.lafkon.net/2008/lac2008/plakat/). because every poster
  will be different it would make sense to have not an offset printrun but
  use laser printing or cad plotting.
  - how is the budget for printing?

  best regards,
  christoph & benjamin

  hi Christoph and Benjamin,

  Sorry for the late reply, I could hardly find time to have a look at this the last
  few days.

  last year we spent 900 eur on printing posters/leaflets, there was :
  - 750x poster 35x50cm offset (178,20 € @ rapid-flyer.com)
  - 14x poster 120x176 digital print (510,69€ @ diazo, local pro printer)
  (these big posters are spread all over Poitiers and in the main festival venues)
  - 5000x flyers Classy (350g+UV) A6 (241,78€ @ flyer.be)

  this year, we've got the same tight budget (approx. 900€). New directions could be
  (not set in stone yet) :
  - we could print a little bit less 35x50 posters, the same for small leaflets (A6)
  - A6 flyer is too small to get enough info/details, a bigger "take-away leaflet"
  with more details would be nice, A4 fold in 2 or 4 for instance (is that something
  you could work on ?)
  - we might print 27 instead of 14 posters 120x176 (it depends if there is space
  left, reply in November)
  - any new proposal for size/price/weight/type of paper/printer is welcome if
  you've got ideas.

  Here is a place where you can fin different versions of GOTO10 and make art logos
  http://samotham.goto10.org/l0g0s/goto10/
  I will provide you the partners logos later (still pending confirmations), but you
  can already consider there will be between 14 and 18 partners logos (to put at the
  bottom).

  the main details to be put on the poster are :
  - make art
  - une semaine dédiée aux mondes du Logiciel Libre et des arts numériques
  - du 7 au 13 décembre 2009
  - Expositions / Concerts / Présentations / Ateliers
  - http://makeart.goto10.org
  - [[a text block (only readable when you're in front of) would be added in a
  corner as last year : http://makeart.goto10.org/2008/?page=press]]

  Currently we can't promise anything about a second travel ticket. Where and how
  would you both come from ?

  Please tell us more if you've got ideas about size/price/weight/type of
  paper/printer company.

  The festival program will be fixed mid-september (hopefully a bit earlier).
  Is it possible for you to send us a preview of the poster+website before end of
  August ?

  all the best,

  Thomas

  >> - 750x poster 35x50cm offset (178,20 € @ rapid-flyer.com)
  >> - 14x poster 120x176 digital print (510,69€ @ diazo, local pro printer)
  >> (these big posters are spread all over Poitiers and in the main
  >> festival venues)
  >> - 5000x flyers Classy (350g+UV) A6 (241,78€ @ flyer.be)
  >>
  >> this year, we've got the same tight budget (approx. 900€). New
  >> directions could be (not set in stone yet) :
  >> - we could print a little bit less 35x50 posters, the same for small
  >> leaflets (A6)
  >> - A6 flyer is too small to get enough info/details, a bigger
  >> "take-away leaflet" with more details would be nice, A4 fold in 2 or 4
  >> for instance (is that something you could work on ?)
  >> - we might print 27 instead of 14 posters 120x176 (it depends if there
  >> is space left, reply in November)
  >> - any new proposal for size/price/weight/type of paper/printer is
  >> welcome if you've got ideas.
  >>
  >> Here is a place where you can fin different versions of GOTO10 and
  >> make art logos
  >> http://samotham.goto10.org/l0g0s/goto10/
  >> I will provide you the partners logos later (still pending
  >> confirmations), but you can already consider there will be between 14
  >> and 18 partners logos (to put at the bottom).
  >>
  >> the main details to be put on the poster are :
  >> - make art
  >> - une semaine dédiée aux mondes du Logiciel Libre et des arts numériques
  >> - du 7 au 13 décembre 2009
  >> - Expositions / Concerts / Présentations / Ateliers
  >> - http://makeart.goto10.org
  >> - [[a text block (only readable when you're in front of) would be
  >> added in a corner as last year :
  >> http://makeart.goto10.org/2008/?page=press]]
  >>
  >> Currently we can't promise anything about a second travel ticket.
  >> Where and how would you both come from ?
  >>
  >> Please tell us more if you've got ideas about size/price/weight/type
  >> of paper/printer company.
  >>
  >> The festival program will be fixed mid-september (hopefully a bit
  >> earlier).
  >> Is it possible for you to send us a preview of the poster+website
  >> before end of August ?
  >>
  >> all the best,

  hi thomas,

  we recently did some research and realised that there is not an
  out-of-the-box easy solution to get the printing done like e.g. flyerwire.
  therefore we recommend the following:

  - you decide on format and number of posters
  - number of flyers
  - you give as a definitive budget (is it inclusive tax/VAT?)
  - deadline

  - we take care of the production, try our best to fit your wishes within
  the budget, send you our proposal beforehand and if everybody is happy,
  take care of the printing and send the posters to poitiers.

  after doing testprints, we regard the following as the best and cheapest
  solution to have the generative posters printed.

  we found a printing shop in essen/germany which offers following conditions:
  ----------------------------------------------------------

  -b/w plots on white paper:

     -- A0: 1,05 €
     -- A1: 0,71 €
     -- A2: 0,46 €

  b/w plots on neon paper:

     -- A0: 3,24 €
     -- A1: 2,35 €
     -- A2: 1,97 €

  b/w plots on coloured paper:

     -- A0: 3,24 €
     -- A1: 2,02 €
     -- A2: 1,34 €

  ----------------------------------------------------------
  here you can download some pictures of the testprints to get an impression:
  http://www.lafkon.net/exchange/makeartwtf_printtests.tar.gz

  we recommend to have a mix of white,green and red paper posters.

  for the flyers we try to find an solution to get the flyers offset
  printed, for having about 10-40 different (generated) flyers.

  still waiting for text and sponsor logos.
  so far for the printing.

  regarding the website:
  how can we commit the design.

  feedback, texts and sponsor logos please asap, because the procedure
  until you have the final posters in poitiers will also take some time
  and there is not much left.


  best regards,
  christoph + benjamin

  hi again,

  before I forget, budget we have is inclusive VAT (we pay it and don't get it refunded)

  == about big posters, I already told you in previous email
  but it's *27* posters 120x176cm for 685€ (and not *23*) at a local pro printer
  (specialised in architect maps and stuffs like that)
  BTW, feel free to tell me if you find cheaper elsewhere else, but then shipping
  costs would be expensive I guess.

  == about regular poster, best prices I found locally were :
  - A3 0,20€ per unit
  - A2 0,62€ per unit is quantity is 500
  A3 are more practical as at many places you can't stick A2 cause it's too big.
  Ideally 500 A3s, but could be less (up to 300?), next to it a small amount of A2
  would be good (20-50).

  == about flyers (recto+verso), it's tricky regarding costs.
  I think A5 could be nice (= recto-verso A4s divived cut at middle).
  At regular printers (not offset) it would be less than 0,03€ per unit for high
  quantities (I don't have the exact figure though). Offset printers would be much
  more expensive it seems (for information, we worked with flyer.be in the past)
  ideally 5000, but could be less (3000?)

  The current budget says we've got 250€ (based on the prices above). Then I'm
  afraid what you suggest would be more expensive or we would have to reduce quantities.
  Could you quickly make a proposal considering what you suggest (different
  colors/papers, printing on your side and shipping it to Poitiers), considering
  above quantities/formats for flyers and regular posters ?

  quick feedback about the last versions :
  - we still find make art logo is not really readable (I mean when you're not in
  just front of it, it's not very obvious to realize that's it's "make art")
  - the basic texts (not the block text at the bottom) are wrong, I already gave it
  to you by email few weeks ago (une semaine dédiée aux mondes du Logiciel Libre et
  des arts numériques, - du 7 au 13 décembre 2009, Expositions / Concerts /
  Présentations / Ateliers)
  note there is a *é* in "Présentations".
  - for the English version it would be exactly :
  "a week dedicated to the world of Free Software and digital art"
  (missing "the" in your version and "art" not "arts")
  "from 7 to 13 December 2009"
  "Exhibition - Concerts - Presentations - Workshops"
  - other than than, we really like them :)

  about the website, claude who's the website maintainer is currently looking at it.
  I'll keep you updated.

  cheers,

  Thomas

  Hi Christoph CC Thomas,

  We would like to pay extra attention to FLOSS design in this years
  make art exhibition, and would like to have a few posters printed on
  heavier quality paper as part of the exhibition (see we really love
  them :). Would you be ok with that? We want to add an explanation
  about your design concept and tools. Next to that we will have prints
  from new work of Olivier Laruelle (who did make art designs in
  previous years). We're dedicating a block of presentations to FLOSS
  design as well, with hopefully a talk by you, a talk by Olivier and a
  talk by Milovann (architect).

  Let us know what you think :)

  I hope you and Thomas can figure out a way to make the printing
  process work (it is a bit of a puzzle with budget and concept both
  needing to fit, but I'm sure you two can find a working solution).

  Marloes

  hi Christoph,

  thank you for all the messages/news. We're getting long to reply cause we're busy
  with other things/projects.

  about the logos/sponsors, I now have the final package ready :
  http://samotham.goto10.org/l0g0s/makeart09
  This is important that you put them in the same order as I put them (number
  ident), I also indicated where to put (very) small separations between different
  groups of partners. Also please note "15" has got 2 different logos.

  about the website, we like it! Good job!
  we just think the logo is weird where/how it is. Maybe putting GOTO10 plain text
  instead of the logo could do? (or keep it in the same area as last year?)
  Could you please commit it on the SVN?
  I'll start filling the website soonish.

  About the poster, we like it like that, great!

  about the *text on the poster*, I put on the SVN the prefinal version (svn
  update). Both EN + FR. When should we tell you how many French/English?
  it is there: '/misc/txt-poster-makeart09.txt'
  I say prefinal cause very minor modifications could be done soon.
  If we make modifications, it will be easy for you to see what using your favorite
  svn/diff client. "Meld" is a nice diff tool if you don't know already.

  about the *texts on the flyer*, it's next to poster : txt-flyer-EN-makeart09.txt
  and txt-flyer-FR-makeart09.txt
  could you just quickly tell me if all this could fit in one A5 page ? We hope you
  can find a nice layout/design that works with it. Otherwise, please tell me and
  i'll shorten it.

  now something important, we noticed you're using Windows when sending emails.
  We were quite disappointed about that...
  However we trust you that you use FLOSS programs only to make the poster/website.
  Could you please confirm us that you'll give a talk using Linux OS when at make art?
  On the same topic, we ask all make art artists to put their source code online
  using a Free licence. Are you going to put online the type of document you
  provided us at the beginning ?

  few more question:
  - would you be ok to get to make art from Friday till Sunday?
  - would you travel from Berlin?
  - have you got precise ideas of what could be shown at make art exhibition
  regarding your works ? (how many prints? size? type of paper? framework or not?)
  please tell us ASAP about that, we need to adjust the budget.

  that's all for now,
  feel free to ask if I forgot something.

  best,

  Thomas

  hi thomas, hi marloes,

   > now something important, we noticed you're using Windows
   > when sending emails.
   > We were quite disappointed about that...

  i will try to work on that.

   > However we trust you that you use FLOSS programs
   > only to make the poster/website.

  what exactly do you mean by trust?
  graphics are generated with processing on gnu/linux,
  posters are layouted with latex on the same machine,
  the whole process takes place in a 100% floss environment.

  while we are investigating the possibilities of floss software
  for design processes and are pretty stunned about these possibilites,
  we never pretended to have a 100% floss tool chain.
  actually we are using gnu/linux, osx AND windows.
  making a living out of being graphic designer includes certain workflows
  at the moment (still) and we are not backed up by any academic or
  cultural funding.
  but we really do not see any need to feel sorry for this.

  the whole source for the poster, including graphics, tools and
  documentation are available under copyleft licenses (gpl,gfdl,cc-by-sa),
  this includes the latex documents, bash scripts and graphics available
  in pdf and svg format.

  http://www.forkable.eu/generators/wtf

  if you are interested in the floss character of the work please have
  a look there instead of email headers.

  if this doesn't comply to your rules, please let us know.

  best regards,
  christoph

  >> too big.

  >>>> we recently did some research and realised that there is not an
  >>>> out-of-the-box easy solution to get the printing done like e.g.
  >>>> flyerwire.
  >>>> therefore we recommend the following:
  >>>>
  >>>> - you decide on format and number of posters
  >>>> - number of flyers
  >>>> - you give as a definitive budget (is it inclusive tax/VAT?)
  >>>> - deadline
  >>>>
  >>>> - we take care of the production, try our best to fit your wishes
  >>>> within
  >>>> the budget, send you our proposal beforehand and if everybody is happy,
  >>>> take care of the printing and send the posters to poitiers.
  >>>>
  >>>> after doing testprints, we regard the following as the best and
  >>>> cheapest
  >>>> solution to have the generative posters printed.
  >>>>
  >>>> we found a printing shop in essen/germany which offers following
  >>>> conditions:
  >>>> ----------------------------------------------------------
  >>>>
  >>>> -b/w plots on white paper:
  >>>>
  >>>>   -- A0: 1,05 €
  >>>>   -- A1: 0,71 €
  >>>>   -- A2: 0,46 €
  >>>>
  >>>> b/w plots on neon paper:
  >>>>
  >>>>   -- A0: 3,24 €
  >>>>   -- A1: 2,35 €
  >>>>   -- A2: 1,97 €
  >>>>
  >>>> b/w plots on coloured paper:
  >>>>
  >>>>   -- A0: 3,24 €
  >>>>   -- A1: 2,02 €
  >>>>   -- A2: 1,34 €
  >>>>
  >>>> ----------------------------------------------------------
  >>>> here you can download some pictures of the testprints to get an
  >>>> impression:
  >>>> http://www.lafkon.net/exchange/makeartwtf_printtests.tar.gz
  >>>>
  >>>> we recommend to have a mix of white,green and red paper posters.
  >>>>
  >>>> for the flyers we try to find an solution to get the flyers offset
  >>>> printed, for having about 10-40 different (generated) flyers.
  >>>>
  >>>> still waiting for text and sponsor logos.
  >>>> so far for the printing.
  >>>>
  >>>> regarding the website:
  >>>> how can we commit the design.
  >>>>
  >>>> feedback, texts and sponsor logos please asap, because the procedure
  >>>> until you have the final posters in poitiers will also take some time
  >>>> and there is not much left.
  >>>>
  >>>>
  >>>> best regards,
  >>>> christoph + benjamin

  Christoph Haag wrote:

  Really sorry about Thomas' clumsy mail... His English is not super
  fluent and he sometimes expresses himself in ways that sound ...
  well... plain wrong :) We don't inspect email headers for a hobby,
  Thomas is just very cautious (and a bit too fanatic) because we've had
  invited artists using windows or OSX in the past during the festival
  (in installations and presentations) and this is of course a pity
  during a festival with such clear emphasis. Hope this explains things!
  We are super excited about your work :)

  Best wishes,
  Marloes

  >
  >  >However we trust you that you use FLOSS programs
  >  >only to make the poster/website.
  >
  > what exactly do you mean by trust?
  > graphics are generated with processing on gnu/linux,
  > posters are layouted with latex on the same machine,
  > the whole process takes place in a 100% floss environment.
  >
  > while we are investigating the possibilities of floss software
  > for design processes and are pretty stunned about these possibilites,
  > we never pretended to have a 100% floss tool chain.
  > actually we are using gnu/linux, osx AND windows.
  > making a living out of being graphic designer includes certain workflows
  > at the moment (still) and we are not backed up by any academic or
  > cultural funding.
  > but we really do not see any need to feel sorry for this.
  >
  > the whole source for the poster, including graphics, tools and
  > documentation are available under copyleft licenses (gpl,gfdl,cc-by-sa),
  > this includes the latex documents, bash scripts and graphics available
  > in pdf and svg format.
  >
  > http://www.forkable.eu/generators/wtf
  >
  > if you are interested in the floss character of the work please have
  > a look there instead of email headers.
  >
  > if this doesn't comply to your rules, please let us know.
  >
  >
  > best regards,
  > christoph

  http://no.systmz.goto10.org

  hi marloes, hi thomas,

  here are the texts.

  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  BIOGRAPHY
  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  Christoph Haag studied design at the Academy of Media Arts Cologne /
  Department of Hybrid Space.
  Benjamin Stephan studied design and computer sciences at the University
  of Applied Sciences Augsburg.

  They are working together as LAFKON since 2001, doing research,
  experimentation and commercially applied design.
  LAFKON is currently based in Augsburg, Germany.

  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  POSTER DESCRIPTION
  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  For Goto10 LAFKON developed generative posters to promote a week
  dedicated to the world of Free Software and digital arts, make art 2009.

  Glued together inside bash scripts, Processing, LaTeX and a bag full
  of GNU/Linux utilities lay the foundation for this scripted design.

  Processing sketches are mostly based on GPL licensed code
  from http://www.openprocessing.org.

  Get the source at http://www.forkable.eu/generators/wtf

  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  TALK DESCRIPTION
  -----------------------------------------------------------------------
  What possibilities does FLOSS offer for graphic design beside
  the replacement of common workflows already known from the
  world of closed-source software?

  Processing, an open source <a href="http://www.processing.org">
  "programming language and integrated development environment (IDE) built
  for the electronic arts and visual design communities"</a>
  meets <a href="http://scienceblogs.com/goodmath/2008/01/the_genius_of_donald_knuth_typ.php">
  software dinosaurs like Donald Knuth's typesetting program TeX</a>
  and the free software Unix shell <a
  href="http://tldp.org/LDP/abs/html/"> Bash </a>.

  The talk will summarize experiences made during practice and give a
  look-out to future plans.

  -----------------------------------------------------------------------


  > next to an image of one of the posters (if you want to select one, you
  > can provide me with the one you prefer, otherwise I take one from the pdf).

  you can include http://www.forkable.eu/generators/wtf/o/fr/A1/random.png
  which delivers a random image or just take one from the pdf.

  just to remind you, posters are not completly finished, please let us
  know when we can start the generator. would you like to have the final
  pdfs as a single file?
  also still waiting for the final ok for the flyer texts.

  > Thanks in advance and thanks for all your hard work!

  thank you!


  best regards,
  christoph

  hi thomas,

  images size is only prescribed in width (300px). i thought that for the
  artist/project pages it's good to decide for each picture individually
    and not to have a forced image format.

  so practically it's up to you. i think the square looks good, but i
  imagine there might be cases where it's hard to find a good clipping. if
  you prefer to go for a consistent format, i think the square is nice.

  i realized that we will have to do some adjustments in the css, for text
  padding mostly.

  best regards,
  christoph

  hello Christoph,

  please find attached the final text to include in the poster and in the flyer
  (recto + verso).

  About these final versions, please note the list of artists was updated, most of
  the text on the verso was modified etc.. about the logo : please remove
  23_serrurerie but add "Lieu Multiple" logo next to Espace Mendès-France
  (15_espace_mendes_france...).

  Quick reminder of expected sizes / printed quantities :
  - 27 posters 120x176cm
  - between 300 and 500 x A3 (42x29,7cm)
  - between 3000 and 5000 x A5 (14,85x21cm)

  for each, I would like one single PDF if possible.

  about the flyer and the 'A4 cut in the middle' trick, actually the printer will do
  it. But they can't guarantee it will be perfect, that's why I found it was not a
  problem to have margin/blank. Cause anyway, there are margins all over.
  But we don't care a lot, and we're a bit late, so just do what is the easiest for you.

  i think that's all. Feel free to ping us if you need more details. If you need a
  quick important feedback from us, please feel free to bother us and we'll try to
  reply ASAP.
  When could it be ready ? as you can imagine, we're a bit late so the sooner the better

  thanks in advance!

  Thomas

  http://www.lafkon.net/exchange/makeart/091113_final.tar.gz

  notice:
  - i added a "concert" before all concerts because actually we lack space
  for a "concerts"-headline and i think these way it's best to get the
  information. i also added the venue for the placard-concert.
  - lieu-multiple is beneath espace-mendes (not next to) also for space
  reason.

  i hope i did not forget something ;)

  > Quick reminder of expected sizes / printed quantities :
  > - 27 posters 120x176cm

  best regards,

  hi Christoph,

  ok good, I double checked with new people and we found some mistakes (mostly our
  fault... but not only ;)

  poster:

  - EN+FR: Koray Tahiroğlu (turkish accent on the "G", if not possible for font
  reason, let's keep it like that)
  - EN+FR: "organisé par" at the bottom is very (too?) small on large posters (A1)
  - FR+EN: about partners logo: don't change anything but just Crédit Agricole that
  you put at the bottom of "Conseil Général" (on the left or "Pulsar" radio)
  - FR+EN: Noyade: Fr > FR (my fault)
  - FR: catchphrase "... aux mondes *du* Logiciel ..." and not *de*
  - FR: for each of the 3 Concerts lines (BTW it's a good idea like this), could you
  do this : Concerts "Placard" (*s* + adding "" for Placard), Concerts "Galactique",
  Concerts "Hardware" ?
  - EN: wrong dates ! (7th-13th instead of 8th-13th!)

  flyer:

  typos and minor changes
  - FR+EN: about taku unami + mattin > you can remove 'to be confirmed'
  - FR+EN: Noyade: Fr > FR (recto artist list)
  - FR+EN: removing "" for Placard
  - FR: remove ", auto-réplication" (unless marloes proposes a replacement)
  - EN: remove ", self replicating" (unless marloes proposes a replacement)
  - FR: "un exposition" > "une exposition" (missing e, my fault...)
  - FR: vendredi 11 décembre à 17h<line_break> => vendredi 11 décembre
  <line_break>17h agents secrets...
  - EN: same as above in the English version
  - FR: 17:00 > 17h - 10:30 > 10h30 (x2) - 14:00 > 14h (x2) - 18:00 > 18h
  - FR: rafraichissantes > rafraichissante (no "s")
  - FR+EN: "Espace Mendès-France" >> "Espace Mendès-France (Lieu Multiple)"

  actually, an easy way to visually check the diff between the version sent few days
  ago and this new one attached, I would advise you to use "meld" diff GUI tool. In
  one glance, you'll get everything.

   > the 27 for the panels in french only i guess,

  yes

   > for the rest how many in english and french?

  about A3 posters:
  - 120 EN
  - 380 FR
  (that's also good to have some extra A2, A1 pdf versions as it would be better for
  some places)

  about flyers
  - 1000 EN
  - 4000 FR

   >> When could it be ready ? as you can imagine, we're a bit late so the
   >> sooner the better
   >
   > if everything goes fine, i think you will have it in 2 days.

  ok good, let me get ready to go the printer!

  hi Christoph,

  about exhibiting your work inside the exihbition, we had the following
  idea (hope you like it ;). We could use the whole big wall for lafkon
  posters, that wall if you remember the place:
  http://makeart.goto10.org/2007/gallery/people/april-4/people-4-april-01-BIS-photo-ludwig_zeller.jpg

  We would stick posters from different sizes all over using regular glue
  (the one we use to stick posters to announce events, = wallpaper glue
  actually). I think it makes sense.

  Then we could print different sizes and fill up the wall only with
  posters. You could provide us some guidelines about the way/order to put
  them next to each other;

  Let me know what you think of that idea and let's get organised (i'll
  have to go back to the printer to print the posters you want to have there).

  Also, did you plan to exhibit an updated version of the howto you
  provided us at the beginning (thinking about wtf_090812.pdf) ?
  it would makes sense

  please let us know and we'll see how we make it happen.
